    89	class PropagateFilter : public rocksdb::CompactionFilter {
    90	 public:
    91	  const char *Name() const override { return "PropagateFilter"; }
    92	  bool Filter([[maybe_unused]] int level, const Slice &key, [[maybe_unused]] const Slice &value,
    93	              [[maybe_unused]] std::string *new_value, [[maybe_unused]] bool *modified) const override {
    94	    // We propagate Lua commands which don't store data,
    95	    // just in order to implement updating Lua state.
    96	    return key == engine::kPropagateScriptCommand;
    97	  }
    98	};

   334	  SetBlobDB(&subkey_opts);
   335	
   336	  rocksdb::BlockBasedTableOptions pubsub_table_opts = InitTableOptions();
   337	  rocksdb::ColumnFamilyOptions pubsub_opts(options);
   338	  pubsub_opts.table_factory.reset(rocksdb::NewBlockBasedTableFactory(pubsub_table_opts));
   339	  pubsub_opts.compaction_filter_factory = std::make_shared<PubSubFilterFactory>();
   340	  pubsub_opts.disable_auto_compactions = config_->rocks_db.disable_auto_compactions;
   341	  SetBlobDB(&pubsub_opts);
   342	
   343	  rocksdb::BlockBasedTableOptions propagate_table_opts = InitTableOptions();
   344	  rocksdb::ColumnFamilyOptions propagate_opts(options);
   345	  propagate_opts.table_factory.reset(rocksdb::NewBlockBasedTableFactory(propagate_table_opts));
   346	  propagate_opts.compaction_filter_factory = std::make_shared<PropagateFilterFactory>();
   347	  propagate_opts.disable_auto_compactions = config_->rocks_db.disable_auto_compactions;
   348	  SetBlobDB(&propagate_opts);
   349	
   350	  rocksdb::BlockBasedTableOptions search_table_opts = InitTableOptions();
   351	  rocksdb::ColumnFamilyOptions search_opts(options);
   352	  search_opts.table_factory.reset(rocksdb::NewBlockBasedTableFactory(search_table_opts));
   353	  search_opts.compaction_filter_factory = std::make_shared<SearchFilterFactory>();
   354	  search_opts.disable_auto_compactions = config_->rocks_db.disable_auto_compactions;
   355	  SetBlobDB(&search_opts);
   356	
   357	  std::vector<rocksdb::ColumnFamilyDescriptor> column_families;
   358	  // Caution: don't change the order of column family, or the handle will be mismatched
   359	  column_families.emplace_back(rocksdb::kDefaultColumnFamilyName, subkey_opts);
   360	  column_families.emplace_back(std::string(kMetadataColumnFamilyName), metadata_opts);
   361	  column_families.emplace_back(std::string(kSecondarySubkeyColumnFamilyName), subkey_opts);
   362	  column_families.emplace_back(std::string(kPubSubColumnFamilyName), pubsub_opts);
   363	  column_families.emplace_back(std::string(kPropagateColumnFamilyName), propagate_opts);
   364	  column_families.emplace_back(std::string(kStreamColumnFamilyName), subkey_opts);
   365	  column_families.emplace_back(std::string(kSearchColumnFamilyName), search_opts);
   366	
   367	  std::vector<std::string> old_column_families;
   368	  auto s = rocksdb::DB::ListColumnFamilies(options, config_->db_dir, &old_column_families);
   369	  if (!s.ok()) return {Status::NotOK, s.ToString()};
   370	
   371	  auto start = std::chrono::high_resolution_clock::now();
   372	  switch (mode) {
   373	    case DBOpenMode::kDBOpenModeDefault: {
   374	      db_ = GET_OR_RET(util::DBOpen(options, config_->db_dir, column_families, &cf_handles_));
   375	      break;
   376	    }
   377	    case DBOpenMode::kDBOpenModeForReadOnly: {
   378	      db_ = GET_OR_RET(util::DBOpenForReadOnly(options, config_->db_dir, column_families, &cf_handles_));
   379	      break;
   380	    }
   381	    case DBOpenMode::kDBOpenModeAsSecondaryInstance: {
   382	      db_ = GET_OR_RET(
   383	          util::DBOpenAsSecondaryInstance(options, config_->db_dir, config_->dir, column_families, &cf_handles_));
   384	      break;
   385	    }
   386	    default:
   387	      unreachable();
   388	  }
   389	  auto end = std::chrono::high_resolution_clock::now();
   390	  int64_t duration = std::chrono::duration_cast<std::chrono::milliseconds>(end - start).count();
   391	
   392	  if (!db_) {
   393	    info("[storage] Failed to load the data from disk: {} ms", duration);
   394	    return {Status::DBOpenErr};
   395	  }
   396	  info("[storage] Success to load the data from disk: {} ms", duration);
   397	
   398	  return Status::OK();
   399	}

    30	enum class IndexOnDataType : uint8_t {
    31	  HASH = kRedisHash,
    32	  JSON = kRedisJson,
    33	};
    34	
    35	inline constexpr auto kErrorInsufficientLength = "insufficient length while decoding metadata";
    36	inline constexpr auto kErrorIncorrectLength = "length is too short or too long to be parsed as a vector";
    37	
    38	class IndexMetadata {
    39	 public:
    40	  uint8_t flag = 0;  // all reserved
    41	  IndexOnDataType on_data_type;
    42	
    43	  std::string_view OnDataTypeName() const { return RedisTypeNames[(size_t)on_data_type]; }
    44	
    45	  void Encode(std::string *dst) const {
    46	    PutFixed8(dst, flag);
    47	    PutFixed8(dst, uint8_t(on_data_type));
    48	  }
    49	
    50	  rocksdb::Status Decode(Slice *input) {
    51	    if (!GetFixed8(input, &flag)) {
    52	      return rocksdb::Status::InvalidArgument(kErrorInsufficientLength);
    53	    }
    54	
    55	    if (!GetFixed8(input, reinterpret_cast<uint8_t *>(&on_data_type))) {
    56	      return rocksdb::Status::InvalidArgument(kErrorInsufficientLength);
    57	    }
    58	
    59	    return rocksdb::Status::OK();
    60	  }
    61	};

   272	struct IndexPrefixes {
   273	  std::vector<std::string> prefixes;
   274	
   275	  static inline const std::string all[] = {""};
   276	
   277	  auto begin() const {  // NOLINT
   278	    return prefixes.empty() ? std::begin(all) : prefixes.data();
   279	  }
   280	
   281	  auto end() const {  // NOLINT
   282	    return prefixes.empty() ? std::end(all) : prefixes.data() + prefixes.size();
   283	  }
   284	
   285	  void Encode(std::string *dst) const {
   286	    for (const auto &prefix : prefixes) {
   287	      PutFixed32(dst, prefix.size());
   288	      dst->append(prefix);
   289	    }
   290	  }
   291	
   292	  rocksdb::Status Decode(Slice *input) {
   293	    uint32_t size = 0;
   294	
   295	    while (GetFixed32(input, &size)) {
   296	      if (input->size() < size) return rocksdb::Status::Corruption(kErrorInsufficientLength);
   297	      prefixes.emplace_back(input->data(), size);
   298	      input->remove_prefix(size);
   299	    }
   300	
   301	    return rocksdb::Status::OK();
   302	  }
   303	};

    34	
    35	bool MetadataFilter::Filter([[maybe_unused]] int level, const Slice &key, const Slice &value,
    36	                            [[maybe_unused]] std::string *new_value, [[maybe_unused]] bool *modified) const {
    37	  Metadata metadata(kRedisNone, false);
    38	  rocksdb::Status s = metadata.Decode(value);
    39	  auto [ns, user_key] = ExtractNamespaceKey(key, stor_->IsSlotIdEncoded());
    40	  if (!s.ok()) {
    41	    warn("[compact_filter/metadata] Failed to decode, namespace: {}, key: {}, err: {}", ns, user_key, s.ToString());
    42	    return false;
    43	  }
    44	  debug("[compact_filter/metadata] namespace: {}, key: {}, result: {}", ns, user_key,
    45	        (metadata.Expired() ? "deleted" : "reserved"));
    46	  return metadata.Expired();
    47	}
    48	
    49	Status SubKeyFilter::GetMetadata(const InternalKey &ikey, Metadata *metadata) const {
    50	  auto db = stor_->GetDB();
    51	  const auto cf_handles = stor_->GetCFHandles();
    52	  // storage close the would delete the column family handler and DB
    53	  if (!db || cf_handles->size() < 2) return {Status::NotOK, "storage is closed"};
    54	  std::string metadata_key = ComposeNamespaceKey(ikey.GetNamespace(), ikey.GetKey(), stor_->IsSlotIdEncoded());
    55	
    56	  if (cached_key_.empty() || metadata_key != cached_key_) {
    57	    std::string bytes;
    58	    rocksdb::Status s = db->Get(rocksdb::ReadOptions(), (*cf_handles)[1], metadata_key, &bytes);
    59	    cached_key_ = std::move(metadata_key);
    60	    if (s.ok()) {
    61	      cached_metadata_ = std::move(bytes);
    62	    } else if (s.IsNotFound()) {
    63	      // metadata was deleted(perhaps compaction or manual)
    64	      // clear the metadata
    65	      cached_metadata_.clear();
    66	      return {Status::NotFound, "metadata is not found"};
    67	    } else {
    68	      cached_key_.clear();
    69	      cached_metadata_.clear();
    70	      return {Status::NotOK, "fetch error: " + s.ToString()};
    71	    }
    72	  }
    73	  // the metadata was not found
    74	  if (cached_metadata_.empty()) return {Status::NotFound, "metadata is not found"};
    75	  // the metadata is cached
    76	  rocksdb::Status s = metadata->Decode(cached_metadata_);
    77	  if (!s.ok()) {
    78	    cached_key_.clear();
    79	    return {Status::NotOK, "decode error: " + s.ToString()};
    80	  }
    81	  return Status::OK();
    82	}
    83	
    84	bool SubKeyFilter::IsMetadataExpired(const InternalKey &ikey, const Metadata &metadata) {
    85	  // lazy delete to avoid race condition between command Expire and subkey Compaction
    86	  // Related issue:https://github.com/apache/kvrocks/issues/1298
    87	  //
    88	  // `util::GetTimeStampMS() - 300000` means extending 5 minutes for expired items,
    89	  // to prevent them from being recycled once they reach the expiration time.
    90	  uint64_t lazy_expired_ts = util::GetTimeStampMS() - 300000;
    91	  return metadata.IsSingleKVType()  // metadata key was overwrite by set command
    92	         || metadata.ExpireAt(lazy_expired_ts) || ikey.GetVersion() != metadata.version;
    93	}
    94	
    95	rocksdb::CompactionFilter::Decision SubKeyFilter::FilterBlobByKey([[maybe_unused]] int level, const Slice &key,
    96	                                                                  [[maybe_unused]] std::string *new_value,
    97	                                                                  [[maybe_unused]] std::string *skip_until) const {
    98	  InternalKey ikey(key, stor_->IsSlotIdEncoded());
    99	  Metadata metadata(kRedisNone, false);
   100	  Status s = GetMetadata(ikey, &metadata);
   101	  if (s.Is<Status::NotFound>()) {
   102	    return rocksdb::CompactionFilter::Decision::kRemove;
   103	  }
   104	  if (!s.IsOK()) {
   105	    error("[compact_filter/subkey] Failed to get metadata, namespace: {}, key: {}, err: {}", ikey.GetNamespace(),
   106	          ikey.GetKey(), s.Msg());
   107	    return rocksdb::CompactionFilter::Decision::kKeep;
   108	  }
   109	  // bitmap will be checked in Filter
   110	  if (metadata.Type() == kRedisBitmap) {
   111	    return rocksdb::CompactionFilter::Decision::kUndetermined;
   112	  }
   113	
   114	  bool result = IsMetadataExpired(ikey, metadata);
   115	  return result ? rocksdb::CompactionFilter::Decision::kRemove : rocksdb::CompactionFilter::Decision::kKeep;
   116	}
   117	
   118	bool SubKeyFilter::Filter([[maybe_unused]] int level, const Slice &key, const Slice &value,
   119	                          [[maybe_unused]] std::string *new_value, [[maybe_unused]] bool *modified) const {
   120	  InternalKey ikey(key, stor_->IsSlotIdEncoded());
   121	  Metadata metadata(kRedisNone, false);
   122	  Status s = GetMetadata(ikey, &metadata);
   123	  if (s.Is<Status::NotFound>()) {
   124	    return true;
   125	  }
   126	  if (!s.IsOK()) {
   127	    error("[compact_filter/subkey] Failed to get metadata, namespace: {}, key: {}, err: {}", ikey.GetNamespace(),
   128	          ikey.GetKey(), s.Msg());
   129	    return false;
   130	  }
   131	
   132	  return IsMetadataExpired(ikey, metadata) || (metadata.Type() == kRedisBitmap && redis::Bitmap::IsEmptySegment(value));
   133	}

    35	// 52 bit for microseconds and 11 bit for counter
    36	const int VersionCounterBits = 11;
    37	
    38	static std::atomic<uint64_t> version_counter_ = 0;
    39	
    40	constexpr const char *kErrMetadataTooShort = "metadata is too short";
    41	
    42	InternalKey::InternalKey(Slice input, bool slot_id_encoded) : slot_id_encoded_(slot_id_encoded) {
    43	  uint32_t key_size = 0;
    44	  uint8_t namespace_size = 0;
    45	  GetFixed8(&input, &namespace_size);
    46	  namespace_ = Slice(input.data(), namespace_size);
    47	  input.remove_prefix(namespace_size);
    48	  if (slot_id_encoded_) {
    49	    GetFixed16(&input, &slotid_);
    50	  }
    51	  GetFixed32(&input, &key_size);
    52	  key_ = Slice(input.data(), key_size);
    53	  input.remove_prefix(key_size);
    54	  GetFixed64(&input, &version_);
    55	  sub_key_ = Slice(input.data(), input.size());
    56	}
    57	
    58	InternalKey::InternalKey(Slice ns_key, Slice sub_key, uint64_t version, bool slot_id_encoded)
    59	    : sub_key_(sub_key), version_(version), slot_id_encoded_(slot_id_encoded) {
    60	  uint8_t namespace_size = 0;
    61	  GetFixed8(&ns_key, &namespace_size);
    62	  namespace_ = Slice(ns_key.data(), namespace_size);
    63	  ns_key.remove_prefix(namespace_size);
    64	  if (slot_id_encoded_) {
    65	    GetFixed16(&ns_key, &slotid_);
    66	  }
    67	  key_ = ns_key;
    68	}
    69	
    70	Slice InternalKey::GetNamespace() const { return namespace_; }
    71	
    72	Slice InternalKey::GetKey() const { return key_; }
    73	
    74	Slice InternalKey::GetSubKey() const { return sub_key_; }
    75	
    76	uint64_t InternalKey::GetVersion() const { return version_; }
    77	
    78	std::string InternalKey::Encode() const {
    79	  std::string out;
    80	  size_t total = 1 + namespace_.size() + 4 + key_.size() + 8 + sub_key_.size();
    81	  if (slot_id_encoded_) {
    82	    total += 2;
    83	  }
    84	  out.resize(total);
    85	  auto buf = out.data();
    86	  buf = EncodeFixed8(buf, static_cast<uint8_t>(namespace_.size()));
    87	  buf = EncodeBuffer(buf, namespace_);
    88	  if (slot_id_encoded_) {
    89	    buf = EncodeFixed16(buf, slotid_);
    90	  }
    91	  buf = EncodeFixed32(buf, static_cast<uint32_t>(key_.size()));
    92	  buf = EncodeBuffer(buf, key_);
    93	  buf = EncodeFixed64(buf, version_);
    94	  EncodeBuffer(buf, sub_key_);
    95	  return out;
    96	}
    97	
    98	bool InternalKey::operator==(const InternalKey &that) const {
    99	  if (namespace_ != this->namespace_) return false;
   100	  if (key_ != that.key_) return false;
   101	  if (sub_key_ != that.sub_key_) return false;
   102	  return version_ == that.version_;
   103	}
   104	
   105	// Must slot encoded
   106	uint16_t ExtractSlotId(Slice ns_key) {
   107	  uint8_t namespace_size = 0;
   108	  GetFixed8(&ns_key, &namespace_size);
   109	  ns_key.remove_prefix(namespace_size);
   110	
   111	  uint16_t slot_id = HASH_SLOTS_SIZE;
   112	  GetFixed16(&ns_key, &slot_id);
   113	  return slot_id;
   114	}
   115	
   116	template <typename T>
   117	std::tuple<T, T> ExtractNamespaceKey(Slice ns_key, bool slot_id_encoded) {
   118	  uint8_t namespace_size = 0;
   119	  GetFixed8(&ns_key, &namespace_size);
   120	  T ns(ns_key.data(), namespace_size);
   121	  ns_key.remove_prefix(namespace_size);
   122	
   123	  if (slot_id_encoded) {
   124	    uint16_t slot_id = 0;
   125	    GetFixed16(&ns_key, &slot_id);
   126	  }
   127	
   128	  T key = {ns_key.data(), ns_key.size()};
   129	  return {ns, key};
   130	}
   131	
   132	template std::tuple<Slice, Slice> ExtractNamespaceKey<Slice>(Slice ns_key, bool slot_id_encoded);
   133	template std::tuple<std::string, std::string> ExtractNamespaceKey<std::string>(Slice ns_key, bool slot_id_encoded);
   134	
   135	std::string ComposeNamespaceKey(const Slice &ns, const Slice &key, bool slot_id_encoded) {
   136	  std::string ns_key;
   137	
   138	  PutFixed8(&ns_key, static_cast<uint8_t>(ns.size()));
   139	  ns_key.append(ns.data(), ns.size());
   140	
   141	  if (slot_id_encoded) {
   142	    auto slot_id = GetSlotIdFromKey(key.ToStringView());
   143	    PutFixed16(&ns_key, slot_id);
   144	  }
   145	
   146	  ns_key.append(key.data(), key.size());
   147	
   148	  return ns_key;
   149	}
   150	
   151	std::string ComposeSlotKeyPrefix(const Slice &ns, int slotid) {
   152	  std::string output;
   153	
   154	  PutFixed8(&output, static_cast<uint8_t>(ns.size()));
   155	  output.append(ns.data(), ns.size());
   156	
   157	  PutFixed16(&output, static_cast<uint16_t>(slotid));
   158	
   159	  return output;
   160	}
   161	
   162	std::string ComposeSlotKeyUpperBound(const Slice &ns, int slotid) { return ComposeSlotKeyPrefix(ns, slotid + 1); }
   163	
   164	Metadata::Metadata(RedisType type, bool generate_version, bool use_64bit_common_field)
   165	    : flags((use_64bit_common_field ? METADATA_64BIT_ENCODING_MASK : 0) | (METADATA_TYPE_MASK & type)),
   166	      expire(0),
   167	      version(generate_version ? generateVersion() : 0),
   168	      size(0) {}
   169	
   170	rocksdb::Status Metadata::Decode(Slice *input) {
   171	  if (!GetFixed8(input, &flags)) {
   172	    return rocksdb::Status::InvalidArgument(kErrMetadataTooShort);
   173	  }
   174	
   175	  if (!GetExpire(input)) {
   176	    return rocksdb::Status::InvalidArgument(kErrMetadataTooShort);
   177	  }
   178	
   179	  if (!IsSingleKVType()) {
   180	    if (input->size() < 8 + CommonEncodedSize()) {
   181	      return rocksdb::Status::InvalidArgument(kErrMetadataTooShort);
   182	    }
   183	    GetFixed64(input, &version);
   184	    GetFixedCommon(input, &size);
   185	  }
   186	
   187	  return rocksdb::Status::OK();
   188	}
   189	
   190	rocksdb::Status Metadata::Decode(Slice input) { return Decode(&input); }
   191	
   192	void Metadata::Encode(std::string *dst) const {
   193	  PutFixed8(dst, flags);
   194	  PutExpire(dst);
   195	  if (!IsSingleKVType()) {
   196	    PutFixed64(dst, version);
   197	    PutFixedCommon(dst, size);
   198	  }
   199	}
   200	
   201	void Metadata::InitVersionCounter() {
   202	  // use random position for initial counter to avoid conflicts,
   203	  // when the slave was promoted as master and the system clock may backoff
   204	  version_counter_ = static_cast<uint64_t>(std::rand());
   205	}
   206	
   207	uint64_t Metadata::generateVersion() {
   208	  uint64_t timestamp = util::GetTimeStampUS();
   209	  uint64_t counter = version_counter_.fetch_add(1);
   210	  return (timestamp << VersionCounterBits) + (counter % (1 << VersionCounterBits));
   211	}
   212	
   213	bool Metadata::operator==(const Metadata &that) const {
   214	  if (flags != that.flags) return false;
   215	  if (expire != that.expire) return false;
   216	  if (!IsSingleKVType()) {
   217	    if (size != that.size) return false;
   218	    if (version != that.version) return false;
   219	  }
   220	  return true;

str_replace_editor insert /testbed/src/storage/compact_filter.cc    --new_str '

bool SearchFilter::Filter([[maybe_unused]] int level, const Slice &key, [[maybe_unused]] const Slice &value,
                          [[maybe_unused]] std::string *new_value, [[maybe_unused]] bool *modified) const {
  if (!stor_) return false;

  // Search CF keys are encoded as: <ns_len><ns><type><index><...>
  // We can check whether the corresponding index metadata still exists in Search CF.
  Slice input(key);
  uint8_t ns_len = 0;
  if (!GetFixed8(&input, &ns_len) || input.size() < ns_len + 1) {
    // Unknown key format, keep it.
    return false;
  }
  Slice ns(input.data(), ns_len);
  input.remove_prefix(ns_len);

  uint8_t type_u8 = 0;
  if (!GetFixed8(&input, &type_u8)) return false;

  // INDEX_META is the root of an index. Never delete it here.
  if (static_cast<redis::SearchSubkeyType>(type_u8) == redis::SearchSubkeyType::INDEX_META) return false;

  // The next element must be the index name as a sized string.
  uint32_t index_len = 0;
  if (!GetFixed32(&input, &index_len) || input.size() < index_len) return false;
  Slice index(input.data(), index_len);

  // Build the index meta key and check its existence.
  redis::SearchKey sk(ns.ToStringView(), index.ToStringView());
  std::string index_meta_key = sk.ConstructIndexMeta();

  auto db = stor_->GetDB();
  if (!db) return false;
  std::string tmp;
  auto s = db->Get(rocksdb::ReadOptions(), stor_->GetCFHandle(ColumnFamilyID::Search), index_meta_key, &tmp);
  return s.IsNotFound();
}

bool SearchFilter::Filter([[maybe_unused]] int level, const Slice &key, [[maybe_unused]] const Slice &value,
                          [[maybe_unused]] std::string *new_value, [[maybe_unused]] bool *modified) const {
  if (!stor_) return false;

  // Search CF keys are encoded as: <ns_len><ns><type><index><...>
  // We can check whether the corresponding index metadata still exists in Search CF.
  Slice input(key);
  uint8_t ns_len = 0;
  if (!GetFixed8(&input, &ns_len) || input.size() < ns_len + 1) {
    // Unknown key format, keep it.
    return false;
  }
  Slice ns(input.data(), ns_len);
  input.remove_prefix(ns_len);

  uint8_t type_u8 = 0;
  if (!GetFixed8(&input, &type_u8)) return false;

  // INDEX_META is the root of an index. Never delete it here.
  if (static_cast<redis::SearchSubkeyType>(type_u8) == redis::SearchSubkeyType::INDEX_META) return false;

  // The next element must be the index name as a sized string.
  uint32_t index_len = 0;
  if (!GetFixed32(&input, &index_len) || input.size() < index_len) return false;
  Slice index(input.data(), index_len);

  // Build the index meta key and check its existence.
  redis::SearchKey sk(ns.ToStringView(), index.ToStringView());
  std::string index_meta_key = sk.ConstructIndexMeta();

  auto db = stor_->GetDB();
  if (!db) return false;
  std::string tmp;
  auto s = db->Get(rocksdb::ReadOptions(), stor_->GetCFHandle(ColumnFamilyID::Search), index_meta_key, &tmp);
  return s.IsNotFound();
}

}

bool SearchFilter::Filter([[maybe_unused]] int level, const Slice &key, [[maybe_unused]] const Slice &value,
                          [[maybe_unused]] std::string *new_value, [[maybe_unused]] bool *modified) const {
  if (!stor_) return false;

  // Search CF keys are encoded as: <ns_len><ns><type><index><...>
  // We can check whether the corresponding index metadata still exists in Search CF.
  Slice input(key);
  uint8_t ns_len = 0;
  if (!GetFixed8(&input, &ns_len) || input.size() < ns_len + 1) {
    // Unknown key format, keep it.
    return false;
  }
  Slice ns(input.data(), ns_len);
  input.remove_prefix(ns_len);

  uint8_t type_u8 = 0;
  if (!GetFixed8(&input, &type_u8)) return false;

  // INDEX_META is the root of an index. Never delete it here.
  if (static_cast<redis::SearchSubkeyType>(type_u8) == redis::SearchSubkeyType::INDEX_META) return false;

  // The next element must be the index name as a sized string.
  uint32_t index_len = 0;
  if (!GetFixed32(&input, &index_len) || input.size() < index_len) return false;
  Slice index(input.data(), index_len);

  // Build the index meta key and check its existence.
  redis::SearchKey sk(ns.ToStringView(), index.ToStringView());
  std::string index_meta_key = sk.ConstructIndexMeta();

  auto db = stor_->GetDB();
  if (!db) return false;
  std::string tmp;
  auto s = db->Get(rocksdb::ReadOptions(), stor_->GetCFHandle(ColumnFamilyID::Search), index_meta_key, &tmp);
  return s.IsNotFound();
}

+bool SearchFilter::Filter([[maybe_unused]] int level, const Slice &key, [[maybe_unused]] const Slice &value,
+                          [[maybe_unused]] std::string *new_value, [[maybe_unused]] bool *modified) const {
+  if (!stor_) return false;
+
+  // Search CF keys are encoded as: <ns_len><ns><type><index><...>
+  // We can check whether the corresponding index metadata still exists in Search CF.
+  Slice input(key);
+  uint8_t ns_len = 0;
+  if (!GetFixed8(&input, &ns_len) || input.size() < ns_len + 1) {
+    // Unknown key format, keep it.
+    return false;
+  }
+  Slice ns(input.data(), ns_len);
+  input.remove_prefix(ns_len);
+
+  uint8_t type_u8 = 0;
+  if (!GetFixed8(&input, &type_u8)) return false;
+
+  // INDEX_META is the root of an index. Never delete it here.
+  if (static_cast<redis::SearchSubkeyType>(type_u8) == redis::SearchSubkeyType::INDEX_META) return false;
+
+  // The next element must be the index name as a sized string.
+  uint32_t index_len = 0;
+  if (!GetFixed32(&input, &index_len) || input.size() < index_len) return false;
+  Slice index(input.data(), index_len);
+
+  // Build the index meta key and check its existence.
+  redis::SearchKey sk(ns.ToStringView(), index.ToStringView());
+  std::string index_meta_key = sk.ConstructIndexMeta();
+
+  auto db = stor_->GetDB();
+  if (!db) return false;
+  std::string tmp;
+  auto s = db->Get(rocksdb::ReadOptions(), stor_->GetCFHandle(ColumnFamilyID::Search), index_meta_key, &tmp);
+  return s.IsNotFound();
+}
+
 }  // namespace engine

+

+  if (static_cast<redis::SearchSubkeyType>(type_u8) == redis::SearchSubkeyType::INDEX_META) return false;

+  // Build the index meta key and check its existence.
+  redis::SearchKey sk(ns.ToStringView(), index.ToStringView());
+  std::string index_meta_key = sk.ConstructIndexMeta();
+
+  auto db = stor_->GetDB();
+  if (!db) return false;
+  std::string tmp;
+  auto s = db->Get(rocksdb::ReadOptions(), stor_->GetCFHandle(ColumnFamilyID::Search), index_meta_key, &tmp);
+  return s.IsNotFound();
+}
+
 }  // namespace engine
